function distanceMatrix(points) {
    const n = points.length;
    const matrix = [];
    
    for (let i = 0; i < n; i++) {
        matrix[i] = [];
        for (let j = 0; j < n; j++) {
            if (i === j) {
                matrix[i][j] = 0;
            } else {
                matrix[i][j] = distance(points[i], points[j], { units: 'kilometers' });
            }
        }
    }
    
    return matrix;
}

const matrix = distanceMatrix(cities);
console.table(matrix);

function transformFeature(feature, options = {}) {
    let result = feature;
    
    // Ú†Ø±Ø®Ø´
    if (options.rotate) {
        result = transformRotate(result, options.rotate, {
            pivot: options.pivot
        });
    }
    
    // Ù…Ù‚ÛŒØ§Ø³
    if (options.scale) {
        result = transformScale(result, options.scale, {
            origin: options.scaleOrigin || 'centroid'
        });
    }
    
    // Ø§Ù†ØªÙ‚Ø§Ù„
    if (options.translate) {
        result = transformTranslate(
            result, 
            options.translate.distance,
            options.translate.direction,
            { units: options.translate.units || 'kilometers' }
        );
    }
    
    return result;
}

const transformed = transformFeature(building, {
    rotate: 45,
    scale: 1.5,
    translate: { distance: 1, direction: 90, units: 'kilometers' }
});

    highQuality: true
});

// â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•
// Ù…Ø­Ø§Ø³Ø¨Ù‡ Ø¯Ø±ØµØ¯ Ú©Ø§Ù‡Ø´
// â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•

function simplifyWithStats(feature, tolerance) {
    const original = feature.geometry.coordinates.flat(Infinity).length / 2;
    const simplified = simplify(feature, { tolerance, highQuality: true });
    const after = simplified.geometry.coordinates.flat(Infinity).length / 2;
    
    return {
        simplified,
        originalPoints: original,
        simplifiedPoints: after,
        reduction: ((original - after) / original * 100).toFixed(1) + '%'
    };
}

const stats = simplifyWithStats(complexLine, 0.02);
console.log(`Ú©Ø§Ù‡Ø´: ${stats.reduction} (${stats.originalPoints} â†’ ${stats.simplifiedPoints})`);

import distance from '@turf/distance';

function findWithinRadius(center, points, radiusKm) {
    return featureCollection(
        points.features.filter(p => {
            const dist = distance(center, p, { units: 'kilometers' });
            return dist <= radiusKm;
        }).map(p => {
            const dist = distance(center, p, { units: 'kilometers' });
            return {
                ...p,
                properties: {
                    ...p.properties,
                    distance: dist
                }
            };
        }).sort((a, b) => a.properties.distance - b.properties.distance)
    );
}

const center = point([51.3890, 35.6892]);
const nearbyHospitals = findWithinRadius(center, hospitals, 5);
console.log('Ø¨ÛŒÙ…Ø§Ø±Ø³ØªØ§Ù†â€ŒÙ‡Ø§ÛŒ Ù†Ø²Ø¯ÛŒÚ© (Ûµ Ú©ÛŒÙ„ÙˆÙ…ØªØ±):', nearbyHospitals.features.length);

// â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•
// K Ù†Ø²Ø¯ÛŒÚ©â€ŒØªØ±ÛŒÙ† Ù‡Ù…Ø³Ø§ÛŒÙ‡
// â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•

function kNearestNeighbors(target, points, k) {
    const withDistance = points.features.map(p => ({
        feature: p,
        distance: distance(target, p, { units: 'kilometers' })
    }));
    
    withDistance.sort((a, b) => a.distance - b.distance);
    
    return featureCollection(
        withDistance.slice(0, k).map(item => ({
            ...item.feature,
            properties: {
                ...item.feature.properties,
                distance: item.distance
            }
        }))
    );
}

const nearest3 = kNearestNeighbors(targetPoint, hospitals, 3);
console.log('Û³ Ø¨ÛŒÙ…Ø§Ø±Ø³ØªØ§Ù† Ù†Ø²Ø¯ÛŒÚ©:');
nearest3.features.forEach((h, i) => {
    console.log(`  ${i + 1}. ${h.properties.name} (${h.properties.distance.toFixed(2)} km)`);
});

function addGridIds(grid) {
    return {
        ...grid,
        features: grid.features.map((cell, index) => ({
            ...cell,
            properties: {
                ...cell.properties,
                id: index,
                row: Math.floor(index / 10),
                col: index % 10
            }
        }))
    };
}

const gridWithIds = addGridIds(squares);

import { featureCollection, point } from '@turf/helpers';
import booleanPointInPolygon from '@turf/boolean-point-in-polygon';

const randomPoints = featureCollection([
    point([51.35, 35.65]),
    point([51.36, 35.66]),
    point([51.40, 35.70]),
    point([51.41, 35.71]),
    point([51.42, 35.72]),
    point([51.45, 35.75])
]);

function countPointsInGrid(grid, points) {
    return {
        ...grid,
        features: grid.features.map(cell => {
            const count = points.features.filter(p => 
                booleanPointInPolygon(p, cell)
            ).length;
            
            return {
                ...cell,
                properties: {
                    ...cell.properties,
                    pointCount: count
                }
            };
        })
    };
}

const gridWithCounts = countPointsInGrid(squares, randomPoints);
gridWithCounts.features.forEach((cell, i) => {
    if (cell.properties.pointCount > 0) {
        console.log(`Ø³Ù„ÙˆÙ„ ${i}: ${cell.properties.pointCount} Ù†Ù‚Ø·Ù‡`);
    }
});

    centroids[c].coords.push(p.geometry.coordinates);

    const avgLat = coords.reduce((sum, p) => sum + p[1], 0) / coords.length;
    console.log(`Ù…Ø±Ú©Ø² Ø®ÙˆØ´Ù‡ ${c}: [${avgLon.toFixed(4)}, ${avgLat.toFixed(4)}]`);

// â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•

function spatialStatistics(fc, property) {
    const values = fc.features.map(f => f.properties[property]).filter(v => v !== undefined);
    const n = values.length;
    
    if (n === 0) return null;
    
    const sum = values.reduce((a, b) => a + b, 0);
    const mean = sum / n;
    const sortedValues = [...values].sort((a, b) => a - b);
    const median = n % 2 === 0 
        ? (sortedValues[n/2 - 1] + sortedValues[n/2]) / 2 
        : sortedValues[Math.floor(n/2)];
    const variance = values.reduce((acc, v) => acc + Math.pow(v - mean, 2), 0) / n;
    const stdDev = Math.sqrt(variance);
    
    return {
        count: n,
        sum,
        mean,
        median,
        min: Math.min(...values),
        max: Math.max(...values),
        range: Math.max(...values) - Math.min(...values),
        variance,
        stdDev,
        coefficientOfVariation: (stdDev / mean) * 100
    };
}

const magStats = spatialStatistics(earthquakes, 'magnitude');
console.log('\nØ¢Ù…Ø§Ø± Ú©Ø§Ù…Ù„:', magStats);

const depthStats = spatialStatistics(earthquakes, 'depth');
console.log('Ø¢Ù…Ø§Ø± Ø¹Ù…Ù‚:', depthStats);

// â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•
// Ø±ÙˆØ´â€ŒÙ‡Ø§ÛŒ Ø·Ø¨Ù‚Ù‡â€ŒØ¨Ù†Ø¯ÛŒ Ø¯Ø§Ø¯Ù‡
// â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•

// Ø¯Ø§Ø¯Ù‡â€ŒÙ‡Ø§ÛŒ Ù†Ù…ÙˆÙ†Ù‡
const values = [12, 15, 18, 22, 25, 28, 35, 42, 55, 68, 75, 85, 92, 105, 120];

// â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•
// Û±. Equal Interval (ÙØ§ØµÙ„Ù‡ Ø¨Ø±Ø§Ø¨Ø±)
// â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•

function equalInterval(values, numClasses) {
    const min = Math.min(...values);
    const max = Math.max(...values);
    const interval = (max - min) / numClasses;
    
    const breaks = [];
    for (let i = 0; i <= numClasses; i++) {
        breaks.push(min + (interval * i));
    }
    
    return breaks;
}

const equalBreaks = equalInterval(values, 5);
console.log('Equal Interval:', equalBreaks);
// [12, 33.6, 55.2, 76.8, 98.4, 120]

// â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•
// Û². Quantile (Ú†Ù†Ø¯Ú©)
// â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•

function quantile(values, numClasses) {
    const sorted = [...values].sort((a, b) => a - b);
    const breaks = [sorted[0]];
    
    for (let i = 1; i < numClasses; i++) {
        const index = Math.floor((i / numClasses) * sorted.length);
        breaks.push(sorted[index]);
    }
    
    breaks.push(sorted[sorted.length - 1]);
    return breaks;
}

const quantileBreaks = quantile(values, 5);
console.log('Quantile:', quantileBreaks);

// â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•
// Û³. Natural Breaks (Jenks)
// â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•

function jenks(values, numClasses) {
    // Ù¾ÛŒØ§Ø¯Ù‡â€ŒØ³Ø§Ø²ÛŒ Ø³Ø§Ø¯Ù‡â€ŒØ´Ø¯Ù‡ Jenks
    const sorted = [...values].sort((a, b) => a - b);
    const n = sorted.length;
    
    if (n <= numClasses) {
        return sorted;
    }
    
    // Ù…Ø§ØªØ±ÛŒØ³â€ŒÙ‡Ø§ÛŒ Ù…Ø­Ø§Ø³Ø¨Ù‡
    const mat1 = Array(n + 1).fill(null).map(() => Array(numClasses + 1).fill(0));
    const mat2 = Array(n + 1).fill(null).map(() => Array(numClasses + 1).fill(Infinity));
    
    for (let i = 1; i <= numClasses; i++) {
        mat1[1][i] = 1;
        mat2[1][i] = 0;
    }
    
    for (let l = 2; l <= n; l++) {
        let s1 = 0, s2 = 0, w = 0;
        
        for (let m = 1; m <= l; m++) {
            const i3 = l - m + 1;
            const val = sorted[i3 - 1];
            s2 += val * val;
            s1 += val;
            w++;
            
            const v = s2 - (s1 * s1) / w;
            const i4 = i3 - 1;
            
            if (i4 !== 0) {
                for (let j = 2; j <= numClasses; j++) {
                    if (mat2[l][j] >= v + mat2[i4][j - 1]) {
                        mat1[l][j] = i3;
                        mat2[l][j] = v + mat2[i4][j - 1];
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        
        mat1[l][1] = 1;
        mat2[l][1] = s2 - (s1 * s1) / w;
    }
    
    // Ø§Ø³ØªØ®Ø±Ø§Ø¬ Ø´Ú©Ø³Øªâ€ŒÙ‡Ø§
    const breaks = [sorted[0]];
    let k = n;
    
    for (let j = numClasses; j >= 2; j--) {
        const id = mat1[k][j] - 1;
        breaks.unshift(sorted[id]);
        k = mat1[k][j] - 1;
    }
    
    breaks.push(sorted[n - 1]);
    return [...new Set(breaks)].sort((a, b) => a - b);
}

const jenksBreaks = jenks(values, 5);
console.log('Jenks:', jenksBreaks);

// â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•
// Û´. Standard Deviation
// â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•

function standardDeviation(values, numStdDevs = 1) {
    const mean = values.reduce((a, b) => a + b, 0) / values.length;
    const variance = values.reduce((acc, v) => acc + Math.pow(v - mean, 2), 0) / values.length;
    const stdDev = Math.sqrt(variance);
    
    const breaks = [];
    for (let i = -numStdDevs; i <= numStdDevs; i++) {
        breaks.push(mean + (i * stdDev));
    }
    
    return {
        breaks,
        mean,
        stdDev
    };
}

const stdDevBreaks = standardDeviation(values, 2);
console.log('Standard Deviation:', stdDevBreaks);

// â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•
// Ø§Ø¹Ù…Ø§Ù„ Ø·Ø¨Ù‚Ù‡â€ŒØ¨Ù†Ø¯ÛŒ Ø¨Ù‡ Features
// â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•

import { featureCollection, polygon } from '@turf/helpers';

const districts = featureCollection([
    polygon([[[0, 0], [1, 0], [1, 1], [0, 1], [0, 0]]], { name: 'A', population: 12000 }),
    polygon([[[1, 0], [2, 0], [2, 1], [1, 1], [1, 0]]], { name: 'B', population: 25000 }),
    polygon([[[0, 1], [1, 1], [1, 2], [0, 2], [0, 1]]], { name: 'C', population: 55000 }),
    polygon([[[1, 1], [2, 1], [2, 2], [1, 2], [1, 1]]], { name: 'D', population: 85000 }),
    polygon([[[2, 0], [3, 0], [3, 1], [2, 1], [2, 0]]], { name: 'E', population: 120000 })
]);

function classifyFeatures(fc, property, breaks, colors) {
    return {
        ...fc,
        features: fc.features.map(feature => {
            const value = feature.properties[property];
            let classIndex = 0;
            
            for (let i = 0; i < breaks.length - 1; i++) {
                if (value >= breaks[i] && value < breaks[i + 1]) {
                    classIndex = i;
                    break;
                }
                if (value >= breaks[breaks.length - 1]) {
                    classIndex = breaks.length - 2;
                }
            }
            
            return {
                ...feature,
                properties: {
                    ...feature.properties,
                    classIndex,
                    classColor: colors[classIndex],
                    classLabel: `${breaks[classIndex].toFixed(0)} - ${breaks[classIndex + 1].toFixed(0)}`
                }
            };
        })
    };
}

const populationValues = districts.features.map(f => f.properties.population);
const popBreaks = equalInterval(populationValues, 4);
const colors = ['#ffffcc', '#a1dab4', '#41b6c4', '#225ea8'];

const classifiedDistricts = classifyFeatures(districts, 'population', popBreaks, colors);

console.log('\nØ·Ø¨Ù‚Ù‡â€ŒØ¨Ù†Ø¯ÛŒ Ø¬Ù…Ø¹ÛŒØª:');
classifiedDistricts.features.forEach(f => {
    console.log(`${f.properties.name}: ${f.properties.population} â†’ ${f.properties.classLabel} (${f.properties.classColor})`);
});

/**
 * ØªØ­Ù„ÛŒÙ„ Ø¯Ø³ØªØ±Ø³ÛŒ Ø¨Ù‡ Ø®Ø¯Ù…Ø§Øª Ø¨Ù‡Ø¯Ø§Ø´ØªÛŒ
 * - ÛŒØ§ÙØªÙ† Ù†Ø²Ø¯ÛŒÚ©â€ŒØªØ±ÛŒÙ† Ø¨ÛŒÙ…Ø§Ø±Ø³ØªØ§Ù†
 * - ØªØ­Ù„ÛŒÙ„ Ù¾ÙˆØ´Ø´ Ø®Ø¯Ù…Ø§Øª
 * - Ø´Ù†Ø§Ø³Ø§ÛŒÛŒ Ù…Ù†Ø§Ø·Ù‚ Ú©Ù…â€ŒØ¨Ø±Ø®ÙˆØ±Ø¯Ø§Ø±

import * as turf from '@turf/turf';

class HealthcareAccessAnalysis {
    constructor(hospitals, populationPoints, studyArea) {
        this.hospitals = hospitals;
        this.populationPoints = populationPoints;
        this.studyArea = studyArea;
    }

    // â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•
    // ØªØ­Ù„ÛŒÙ„ Ù†Ø²Ø¯ÛŒÚ©â€ŒØªØ±ÛŒÙ† Ø¨ÛŒÙ…Ø§Ø±Ø³ØªØ§Ù† Ø¨Ø±Ø§ÛŒ Ù‡Ø± Ù†Ù‚Ø·Ù‡ Ø¬Ù…Ø¹ÛŒØªÛŒ
    // â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•
    
    findNearestHospital() {
        return turf.featureCollection(
            this.populationPoints.features.map(pop => {
                const nearest = turf.nearestPoint(pop, this.hospitals);
                const distance = turf.distance(pop, nearest, { units: 'kilometers' });
                
                return {
                    ...pop,
                    properties: {
                        ...pop.properties,
                        nearestHospital: nearest.properties.name,
                        distanceToHospital: Math.round(distance * 100) / 100,
                        hospitalBeds: nearest.properties.beds
                    }
                };
            })
        );
    }

    // â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•
    // Ø§ÛŒØ¬Ø§Ø¯ Ù…Ù†Ø§Ø·Ù‚ Ø®Ø¯Ù…Ø§Øªâ€ŒØ±Ø³Ø§Ù†ÛŒ (Service Areas)
    // â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•
    
    createServiceAreas(distances = [1, 3, 5]) {
        const serviceAreas = [];
        
        this.hospitals.features.forEach(hospital => {
            distances.forEach(dist => {
                const buffer = turf.buffer(hospital, dist, { units: 'kilometers' });
                buffer.properties = {
                    hospitalName: hospital.properties.name,
                    serviceRadius: dist,
                    type: `${dist}km service area`
                };
                serviceAreas.push(buffer);
            });
        });
        
        return turf.featureCollection(serviceAreas);
    }

    // â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•
    // ØªØ­Ù„ÛŒÙ„ Voronoi Ø¨Ø±Ø§ÛŒ ØªØ¹ÛŒÛŒÙ† Ø­ÙˆØ²Ù‡ Ù‡Ø± Ø¨ÛŒÙ…Ø§Ø±Ø³ØªØ§Ù†
    // â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•
    
    createCatchmentAreas() {
        const bbox = turf.bbox(this.studyArea);
        const voronoi = turf.voronoi(this.hospitals, { bbox });
        
        // Ø¨Ø±Ø´ Ø¨Ø§ Ù…Ø­Ø¯ÙˆØ¯Ù‡ Ù…Ø·Ø§Ù„Ø¹Ù‡
        return turf.featureCollection(
            voronoi.features.map((cell, index) => {
                const clipped = turf.intersect(cell, this.studyArea);
                if (clipped) {
                    clipped.properties = {
                        ...this.hospitals.features[index].properties,
                        type: 'catchment'
                    };
                }
                return clipped;
            }).filter(f => f !== null)
        );
    }

    // â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•
    // Ø´Ù†Ø§Ø³Ø§ÛŒÛŒ Ù…Ù†Ø§Ø·Ù‚ Ú©Ù…â€ŒØ¨Ø±Ø®ÙˆØ±Ø¯Ø§Ø±
    // â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•
    
    findUnderservedAreas(maxDistance = 5) {

    // â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•

            grid: densityGrid,
            stats: {
                maxDensity,
                avgDensity: avgDensity.toFixed(2),
                zeroDensityCells,
                zeroDensityPercent: ((zeroDensityCells / counts.length) * 100).toFixed(1)
            }
        };

    analyzeStationSpacing() {
        const distances = [];
        
        this.stations.features.forEach((station, i) => {
            // ÛŒØ§ÙØªÙ† Ù†Ø²Ø¯ÛŒÚ©â€ŒØªØ±ÛŒÙ† Ø§ÛŒØ³ØªÚ¯Ø§Ù‡ Ø¯ÛŒÚ¯Ø±

                this.stations.features.filter((_, j) => i !== j)
            );
            
            if (otherStations.features.length > 0) {
                const nearest = turf.nearestPoint(station, otherStations);
                const distance = turf.distance(station, nearest, { units: 'kilometers' });
                
                distances.push({
                    station: station.properties.name,
                    nearestStation: nearest.properties.name,
                    distance: Math.round(distance * 100) / 100
                });
            }
        });
        
        const distanceValues = distances.map(d => d.distance);
        
        return {
            pairs: distances,
            stats: {
                minSpacing: Math.min(...distanceValues).toFixed(2),
                maxSpacing: Math.max(...distanceValues).toFixed(2),
                avgSpacing: (distanceValues.reduce((a, b) => a + b, 0) / distanceValues.length).toFixed(2)
            }
        };
    }

    analyzeRoutes() {
        return this.routes.features.map(route => {
            const length = turf.length(route, { units: 'kilometers' });
            const bbox = turf.bbox(route);
            const coords = route.geometry.coordinates;
            
            // Ø´Ù…Ø§Ø±Ø´ Ø§ÛŒØ³ØªÚ¯Ø§Ù‡â€ŒÙ‡Ø§ÛŒ Ø±ÙˆÛŒ Ù…Ø³ÛŒØ±
            const stationsOnRoute = this.stations.features.filter(station => {
                const distance = turf.pointToLineDistance(station, route, { units: 'meters' });
                return distance < 50; // ÛµÛ° Ù…ØªØ± ÙØ§ØµÙ„Ù‡ Ù…Ø¬Ø§Ø²
            });

                name: route.properties.name,
                length: length.toFixed(2),
                stationCount: stationsOnRoute.length,

                endPoint: coords[coords.length - 1],
                bbox
            };
        });

    // â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•
    
    generateReport() {
        const coverage500m = this.analyzeStationCoverage(0.5);
        const coverage1km = this.analyzeStationCoverage(1);
        const deserts = this.findTransitDeserts(0.5);
        const density = this.analyzeStationDensity(1);
        const spacing = this.analyzeStationSpacing();
        const suggestions = this.suggestNewStations(3);
        
        return {
            summary: {
                totalStations: this.stations.features.length,
                totalRoutes: this.routes.features.length,
                coverage500m: coverage500m.coveragePercent + '%',
                coverage1km: coverage1km.coveragePercent + '%',
                transitDesertPercent: deserts.desertPercent + '%'
            },
            coverage: { '500m': coverage500m, '1km': coverage1km },
            transitDeserts: deserts,
            density: density.stats,
            spacing: spacing.stats,
            suggestions: suggestions.suggestions?.features?.length || 0,
            timestamp: new Date().toISOString()
        };
    }
}
